### [192] [Alkaid: Resilience to Edit Errors in Provably Secure Steganography via Distance-Constrained Encoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06169)
*Zhihan Cao,Gaolei Li,Jun Wu,Jianhua Li,Hang Zhang,Mingzhe Chen*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: Alkaid是一种可证明安全的隐写方案，通过距离约束编码实现对编辑错误（插入、删除、替换）的鲁棒性，在保持安全性的同时提供确定性错误恢复能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可证明安全的隐写系统虽然提供强隐蔽性，但在现实世界中容易受到编辑错误的影响，因为其解码依赖于完美同步且缺乏纠错能力。

Method: 通过距离约束编码将最小距离解码原则直接集成到编码过程中，强制不同消息的码字之间保持严格的编辑距离下界。如果候选码字违反这个界限，它们会被合并以表示相同消息，从而保证可靠恢复。采用分块和批量处理实现高效实现。

Result: Alkaid在不同错误信道下实现了99%到100%的解码成功率，提供每token 0.2比特的有效载荷以实现高嵌入容量，编码速度为每秒6.72比特，在鲁棒性、容量和效率方面显著超越现有最先进方法。

Conclusion: Alkaid成功地将可证明安全性与编辑错误鲁棒性相结合，通过距离约束编码实现了既安全又可靠的隐写系统，为实际应用中的隐写通信提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: While provably secure steganography provides strong concealment by ensuring stego carriers are indistinguishable from natural samples, such systems remain vulnerable to real-world edit errors (e.g., insertions, deletions, substitutions) because their decoding depends on perfect synchronization and lacks error-correcting capability. To bridge this gap, we propose Alkaid, a provably secure steganographic scheme resilient to edit errors via distance-constrained encoding. The key innovation integrates the minimum distance decoding principle directly into the encoding process by enforcing a strict lower bound on the edit distance between codewords of different messages. Specifically, if two candidate codewords violate this bound, they are merged to represent the same message, thereby guaranteeing reliable recovery. While maintaining provable security, we theoretically prove that Alkaid offers deterministic robustness against bounded errors. To implement this scheme efficiently, we adopt block-wise and batch processing. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Alkaid achieves decoding success rates of 99\% to 100\% across diverse error channels, delivers a payload of 0.2 bits per token for high embedding capacity, and maintains an encoding speed of 6.72 bits per second, significantly surpassing state-of-the-art (SOTA) methods in robustness, capacity, and efficiency.

</details>


### [193] [Designing Trustworthy Layered Attestations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06326)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用分层证明结构，逐层报告目标系统组件的证据；通过结构化目标系统来限制关键组件集合；基于TPM等硬件和Linux+SELinux等软件构建示例系统；提出指导系统开发的若干原则；最后扩展到使用AMD SEV-SNP机密计算硬件。

Conclusion: 分层结构化证明方法能够显著提高系统证明的可靠性，通过限制关键组件集合和逐层证据报告，即使在面对强大攻击者时也能提供可信证明。该方法具有实际可行性，性能开销可接受，且可扩展到不同的硬件平台。

Abstract: Attestation means providing evidence that a remote target system is worthy of trust for some sensitive interaction. Although attestation is already used in network access control, security management, and trusted execution environments, it mainly concerns only a few system components. A clever adversary might manipulate these shallow attestations to mislead the relying party.
  Reliable attestations require layering. We construct attestations whose layers report evidence about successive components of the target system. Reliability also requires structuring the target system so only a limited set of components matters.
  We show how to structure an example system for reliable attestations despite a well-defined, relatively strong adversary. It is based on widely available hardware, such as Trusted Platform Modules, and software, such as Linux with SELinux. We isolate our principles in a few maxims that guide system development. We provide a cogent analysis of our mechanisms against our adversary model, as well as an empirical appraisal of the resulting system. We also identify two improvements to the mechanisms so attestation can succeed against strengthened adversaries. The performance burden of our attestation is negligible, circa 1.3 percent.
  After our first example, we vary our application level, and then also its underlying hardware anchor to use confidential computing with AMD's SEV-SNP. The same maxims help us achieve trustworthy attestations.

  In this paper, we address these challenges by introducing SIABENCH, an agentic evaluation framework for security incident analysis. First, we construct a first-of-its-kind dataset comprising two major SIA task categories: (i) deep analysis workflows for security incidents (25 scenarios) and (ii) alert-triage tasks (135 scenarios). Second, we implement an agent capable of autonomously performing a broad spectrum of SIA tasks (including network and memory forensics, malware analysis across binary/code/PDF formats, phishing email and kit analysis, log analysis, and false-alert detection). ### [195] [Proteus: A Practical Framework for Privacy-Preserving Device Logs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06540)
*Sanket Goutam,Hunter Kippen,Mike Grace,Amir Rahmati*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: Proteus是一个隐私保护的设备日志框架，通过两层方案（哈希假名化和时间轮转加密）在保护PII的同时保持数据分析有效性，支持时间受限的共享访问。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 设备日志在取证调查、企业监控和欺诈检测中至关重要，但导出供第三方分析时经常泄露个人身份信息（PII）。现有方法要么无法在所有日志收集和分析阶段最小化PII暴露，要么牺牲数据保真度，导致分析效果降低。

Method: Proteus采用两层方案：1）对PII字段使用密钥哈希假名化；2）时间轮转加密配合棘轮式临时密钥，防止多快照关联。通过导出棘轮状态实现时间受限的受控共享，允许解密假名化令牌以支持关联和时间线重建，同时不暴露底层PII。后续棘轮轮转确保前向保密，基于DICE的认证验证设备来源。

Result: 在Android logcat上实现Proteus，并在三代硬件上评估。结果显示每条消息的中位延迟为0.2毫秒，每个PII字段的平均大小开销仅为97.1字节。

Conclusion: Proteus能够在面对访问多个日志文件快照的对手时，实现隐私保护的设备日志记录，既不会泄露明文PII，也不会损害数据保真度，支持有效的取证分析。

Abstract: Device logs are essential for forensic investigations, enterprise monitoring, and fraud detection; however, they often leak personally identifiable information (PII) when exported for third-party analysis. Existing approaches either fail to minimize PII exposure across all stages of log collection and analysis or sacrifice data fidelity, resulting in less effective analysis. We present Proteus, a privacy-preserving device logging framework that enables forensic analysis without disclosing plaintext PII or compromising fidelity, even when facing adversaries with access to multiple snapshots of the log files. To achieve this, Proteus proposes a two-layer scheme that employs keyed-hash pseudonymization of PII fields and time-rotating encryption with ratcheted ephemeral keys to prevent multi-snapshot correlation. For controlled sharing, clients export ratchet states that grant time-bounded access, permitting decryption of pseudonymized tokens that enable linkage and timeline reconstruction without exposing the underlying PII. Subsequent ratchet rotations ensure forward secrecy, while DICE-based attestation authenticates device provenance. We implement Proteus as a transparent extension to Android's logcat and evaluate it across three generations of hardware. Our results demonstrate a median latency of 0.2 ms per message and an average per-PII-field size overhead of only 97.1 bytes.

</details>

### [196] [Tool-Genesis: A Task-Driven Tool Creation Benchmark for Self-Evolving Language Agent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05578)
*Bowei Xia,Mengkang Hu,Shijian Wang,Jiarui Jin,Wenxiang Jiao,Yuan Lu,Kexin Li,Ping Luo*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: Tool-Genesis：一个诊断性基准测试，用于量化语言智能体在无预设规范下从抽象需求创建工具的能力，涵盖接口合规性、功能正确性和下游效用等多个维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试主要依赖预定义规范，限制了可扩展性并阻碍了真正的自主演化。虽然最近的研究尝试动态生成工具，但主要强调下游性能，导致"黑盒"评估难以将失败归因于特定原因。

Method: 提出Tool-Genesis诊断基准，评估智能体能否仅从抽象需求（无预设规范）构建任务相关工具，并用它们解决现实问题。该基准量化智能体在接口合规性、功能正确性和下游效用等多个维度的能力。

Result: 研究发现，即使最先进的模型也难以在一次性设置中产生精确的工具接口或可执行逻辑。这些微小的初始缺陷在管道中被放大，导致下游指标急剧下降。

Conclusion: Tool-Genesis将指导未来研究，训练和引导模型合成持久、通用的工具，以更好地应对现实世界挑战。

Abstract: Research on self-evolving language agents has accelerated, drawing increasing attention to their ability to create, adapt, and maintain tools from task requirements. However, existing benchmarks predominantly rely on predefined specifications, which limits scalability and hinders truly autonomous evolution. While recent studies attempt to dynamically generate tools, they primarily emphasize downstream performance, resulting in a "black-box" evaluation that makes it difficult to attribute failures to specific causes. To address this, we propose Tool-Genesis, a diagnostic benchmark designed to quantify agent capabilities across multiple dimensions, including interface compliance, functional correctness, and downstream utility. Tool-Genesis evaluates whether agents can construct task-relevant tools solely from abstract requirements (without preset specifications) and use them to solve realistic problems. Crucially, we find that even state-of-the-art models struggle to produce precise tool interfaces or executable logic in a one-shot setting. These minor initial flaws are amplified through the pipeline, leading to a sharp degradation in downstream metrics. We hope Tool-Genesis will guide future research toward training and steering models to synthesize persistent, general-purpose tools that better address real-world challenges.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该研究为研究人员和实践者提供了可操作的见解，有助于开发更鲁棒、可靠和安全的基于MCP的AI软件系统，填补了该领域系统性故障理解的空白。

Abstract: The rapid adoption of foundation models has significantly expanded the capabilities of software systems, enabling them to perform complex language, reasoning, and interaction tasks that were previously difficult to automate. However, this progress has also introduced novel challenges that were largely absent in previous generations of software. In particular, the increasing integration of foundation models with external tools and resources raises new concerns regarding reliability, security, and robustness. The Model Context Protocol (MCP) has recently been proposed to standardize interactions between AI-based software systems, software tools, and external resources. Despite its growing adoption, there remains limited systematic understanding of real-world faults in MCP-based software systems.
  In this paper, we present the first large-scale taxonomy of faults in MCP servers, comprising five high-level fault categories derived from empirical evidence. To evaluate the completeness and generalizability of this taxonomy, we conduct a survey of MCP practitioners with diverse roles and experience levels. The results confirm that all identified fault categories occur in practice and reveal distinct characteristics that differentiate MCP-specific faults from non-MCP faults.
  Overall, this study provides actionable insights for researchers and practitioners by identifying the most error-prone and critical components of MCP-based systems. These insights can inform the development of more robust, reliable, and secure AI-enabled software systems that rely on MCP.

### [198] [Balancing Latency and Accuracy of Code Completion via Local-Cloud Model Cascading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05974)
*Hanzhen Lu,Lishui Fan,Jiachi Chen,Qiuyuan Chen,Zhao Wei,Zhongxin Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: MCCom是一个用于代码补全的模型级联框架，通过本地小模型与云端大模型的协同工作，在保持高质量的同时显著降低延迟和计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码补全方法存在权衡：大语言模型(LLM)质量高但延迟大，小语言模型(SLM)速度快但效果差。需要一种能平衡准确性和延迟的解决方案。

Method: 提出MCCom框架，级联本地SLM与云端LLM。利用用户行为作为触发信号，仅在SLM失败时调用LLM。采用两阶段推测解码策略和迭代检索机制增强模型协作。训练了一个121M参数的轻量级模型。

Result: 在RepoEval和新的真实基准StmtEval上评估，MCCom将推理延迟降低47.9%，LLM使用量减少46.3%，同时通过有效协作将LLM的精确匹配率提高8.9%。轻量级模型达到7B SOTA模型73.8%的性能。

Conclusion: MCCom通过创新的模型级联框架有效解决了代码补全中准确性与延迟的权衡问题，为实际应用提供了高效实用的解决方案。

Abstract: Line-level code completion requires a critical balance between high accuracy and low latency. Existing methods suffer from a trade-off: large language models (LLMs) provide high-quality suggestions but incur high latency, while small language models (SLMs) are fast but often suboptimal. We propose MCCom (Model-Cascading-based code Completion), a framework that cascades a local SLM with a cloud-based LLM. To achieve effective cascading, MCCom leverages user actions as a novel signal to trigger the LLM only when the SLM fails, significantly reducing cloud computation costs. Furthermore, we introduce a two-stage speculative decoding strategy and an iterative retrieval mechanism to enhance collaboration between the models. We also train a 121M-parameter lightweight model, which achieves 73.8% of the performance of a 7B state-of-the-art model. Evaluated on RepoEval and a new real-world benchmark StmtEval, MCCom reduces inference latency by up to 47.9% and LLM usage by 46.3%, while improving the LLM's exact match rate by 8.9% through effective collaboration.

### [199] [Detecting Semantic Alignments between Textual Specifications and Domain Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06037)
*Shwetali Shimangaud,Lola Burgueño,Rijul Saini,Jörg Kienzle*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种使用NLP和LLM技术评估领域模型与文本规范对齐程度的方法，能够以高精度识别模型元素的对齐、未对齐或未分类状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在软件工程早期阶段，从文本规范中推导出正确的领域模型并建立清晰的链接是一项具有挑战性的任务，特别是对于新手建模者。需要一种能够自动评估模型与规范对齐程度的方法。

Method: 使用自然语言处理技术预处理文本，为每个模型元素生成人工自然语言规范描述，然后使用大型语言模型将生成的描述与原始规范中的匹配句子进行比较。算法将每个模型元素分类为对齐（正确）、未对齐（不正确）或未分类（证据不足），并输出提供分类证据的相关句子。

Result: 在文献中的示例集和通过突变系统生成的错误模型上评估，结果显示能够以接近1的精度和约78%的召回率识别对齐和未对齐情况，每个模型元素的执行时间在18秒到1分钟之间。

Conclusion: 由于算法几乎不会错误分类模型元素，并且能够分类超过3/4的模型元素，因此可以集成到建模工具中提供积极反馈或生成警告，或用于离线验证和质量评估。

Abstract: Context: Having domain models derived from textual specifications has proven to be very useful in the early phases of software engineering. However, creating correct domain models and establishing clear links with the textual specification is a challenging task, especially for novice modelers. Objectives: We propose an approach for determining the alignment between a partial domain model and a textual specification. Methods: To this aim, we use Natural Language Processing techniques to pre-process the text, generate an artificial natural language specification for each model element, and then use an LLM to compare the generated description with matched sentences from the original specification. Ultimately, our algorithm classifies each model element as either aligned (i.e., correct), misaligned (i.e., incorrect), or unclassified (i.e., insufficient evidence). Furthermore, it outputs the related sentences from the textual specification that provide the evidence for the determined class. Results: We have evaluated our approach on a set of examples from the literature containing diverse domains, each consisting of a textual specification and a reference domain model, as well as on models containing modeling errors that were systematically derived from the correct models through mutation. Our results show that we are able to identify alignments and misalignments with a precision close to 1 and a recall of approximately 78%, with execution times ranging from 18 seconds to 1 minute per model element. Conclusion: Since our algorithm almost never classifies model elements incorrectly, and is able to classify over 3/4 of the model elements, it could be integrated into a modeling tool to provide positive feedback or generate warnings, or employed for offline validation and quality assessment.

### [200] [Real-World Fault Detection for C-Extended Python Projects with Automated Unit Test Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06107)
*Lucas Berg,Lukas Krodinger,Stephan Lukasczyk,Annibale Panichella,Gordon Fraser,Wim Vanhoof,Xavier Devroey*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出了一种通过子进程执行来分离测试生成与执行阶段的方法，以解决Python C扩展中异常导致解释器崩溃的问题，从而能够检测故障、生成可重现的测试用例并继续测试非崩溃代码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Python库使用C扩展提升性能，但C代码中的异常会绕过Python异常处理导致解释器崩溃。这些崩溃是真实故障，但自动化测试生成工具会因此完全停止，无法检测或重现底层错误，也无法覆盖非崩溃部分的代码。

Method: 将测试生成与执行阶段分离，改造Pynguin（Python自动化测试生成工具）使用子进程执行。每个生成的测试在隔离的子进程中运行，防止崩溃中断整个测试生成过程。

Result: 在包含21个流行Python库的1648个模块数据集上评估，子进程执行使自动化测试模块数增加最多56.5%，发现了213个独特的崩溃原因，揭示了32个先前未知的故障。

Conclusion: 子进程执行方法有效解决了C扩展崩溃导致测试过程中断的问题，能够检测故障、生成可重现测试用例、研究底层故障，并支持非崩溃代码的测试生成。

Abstract: Many popular Python libraries use C-extensions for performance-critical operations allowing users to combine the best of the two worlds: The simplicity and versatility of Python and the performance of C. A drawback of this approach is that exceptions raised in C can bypass Python's exception handling and cause the entire interpreter to crash. These crashes are real faults if they occur when calling a public API. While automated test generation should, in principle, detect such faults, crashes in native code can halt the test process entirely, preventing detection or reproduction of the underlying errors and inhibiting coverage of non-crashing parts of the code. To overcome this problem, we propose separating the generation and execution stages of the test-generation process. We therefore adapt Pynguin, an automated test case generation tool for Python, to use subprocess-execution. Executing each generated test in an isolated subprocess prevents a crash from halting the test generation process itself. This allows us to (1) detect such faults, (2) generate reproducible crash-revealing test cases for them, (3) allow studying the underlying faults, and (4) enable test generation for non-crashing parts of the code. To evaluate our approach, we created a dataset consisting of 1648 modules from 21 popular Python libraries with C-extensions. Subprocess-execution allowed automated testing of up to 56.5% more modules and discovered 213 unique crash causes, revealing 32 previously unknown faults.

### [201] [Can Adjusting Hyperparameters Lead to Green Deep Learning: An Empirical Study on Correlations between Hyperparameters and Energy Consumption of Deep Learning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06195)
*Taoran Wang,Yanhui Li,Mingliang Ma,Lin Chen,Yuming Zhou*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出从超参数角度分析深度学习模型能耗的新视角，通过实验证明超参数调整能显著影响能耗，适当调整可实现绿色深度学习模型


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着深度学习模型发展，数据集增大和模型结构复杂化导致计算资源和能耗急剧上升，需要关注绿色深度学习模型。本文从超参数对能耗影响的新视角出发，研究如何通过超参数调整降低深度学习能耗

Method: 使用变异算子模拟实践者调整超参数（如训练轮数和学习率），分别训练原始模型和变异模型，收集能耗信息和运行时性能指标，特别关注并行训练多个DL模型的场景

Result: 在五个真实世界DL模型上进行广泛实验，结果显示：(1) 许多超参数与能耗存在正负相关性；(2) 调整超参数可使DL模型更绿色，即在保持性能的同时降低能耗；(3) 在并行环境中，能耗对变化更加敏感

Abstract: Context: Along with developing Deep learning (DL) models, larger datasets and more complex model structures are applied, leading to rising computing resources and energy consumption, which is an alert that green DL models should receive more attention. Objective: This paper focuses on a novel view to analyze DL energy consumption: the effect of hyperparameters on the energy cost of DL models. Method: Our approach involves using mutation operators to simulate how practitioners adjust hyperparameters, such as epochs and learning rates. We train the original and mutated models separately and gather energy information and run-time performance metrics. Moreover, we focus on the parallel scenario where multiple DL models are trained in parallel. Results: To examine the effect of hyperparameters on energy consumption, we conducted extensive experiments on five real-world DL models. The results show that (1) many hyperparameters studied have a (positive or negative) correlation with energy consumption, (2) adjusting hyperparameters can make DL models greener, i.e., lead to less energy consumption without performance damage, and (3) in a parallel environment, energy consumption becomes more susceptible to change. Conclusions: We suggest that hyperparameters need more attention in developing DL models, as appropriately adjusting hyperparameters would cause green DL models.

### [202] [Story Point Estimation Using Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06276)
*Pranam Prakash Shetty,Adarsh Balakrishnan,Mengqiao Xu,Xiaoyin Xi,Zhe Yu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: LLMs在零样本和少样本情况下都能有效预测故事点，性能优于需要大量训练数据的监督深度学习模型，且比较判断可作为少样本示例提升预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统机器学习方法需要大量带标注的训练数据才能有效预测故事点，这在实际项目中难以获得。研究探索LLMs是否能在无训练数据或仅有少量数据的情况下进行准确预测，并研究比较判断是否比直接估计故事点更容易预测。

Method: 使用四种LLMs在16个软件项目上进行实验，采用零样本提示（无训练数据）和少样本提示（少量训练示例）两种方式预测故事点。同时研究比较判断的预测难度以及比较判断能否作为少样本示例提升故事点预测性能。

Result: 零样本提示下，LLMs的预测性能优于使用80%数据训练的监督深度学习模型。少样本提示可进一步提升LLMs性能。比较判断并不比直接估计故事点更容易预测，但比较判断可作为少样本示例有效提升LLMs的预测性能。

Conclusion: LLMs在故事点估计任务中展现出强大潜力，特别是在数据稀缺场景下。比较判断虽不更易预测，但可作为有效的少样本学习材料，为实际软件开发中的敏捷估算提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: This study investigates the use of large language models (LLMs) for story point estimation. Story points are unitless, project-specific effort estimates that help developers on the scrum team forecast which product backlog items they plan to complete in a sprint. To facilitate this process, machine learning models, especially deep neural networks, have been applied to predict the story points based on the title and description of each item. However, such machine learning models require sufficient amounts of training data (with ground truth story points annotated by human developers) from the same software project to achieve decent prediction performance. This motivated us to explore whether LLMs are capable of (RQ1) predicting story points without training data or (RQ2) with only a few training data points. Our empirical results with four LLMs on 16 software projects show that, without any training data (zero-shot prompting), LLMs can predict story points better than supervised deep learning models trained on 80% of the data. The prediction performance of LLMs can be further improved with a few training examples (few-shot prompting). In addition, a recent study explored the use of comparative judgments (between a given pair of items which one requires more effort to implement) instead of directly annotating the story points to reduce the cognitive burden on developers. Therefore, this study also explores (RQ3) whether comparative judgments are easier to predict than story points for LLMs and (RQ4) whether comparative judgments can serve as few-shot examples for LLMs to improve their predictions of story points. Empirical results suggest that it is not easier for LLMs to predict comparative judgments than to directly estimate the story points, but comparative judgments can serve as few-shot examples to improve the LLMs' prediction performance as well as the human-annotated story points.

We conjecture that our proposed general feature model advances the field around Digital Twins by facilitating informed decision-making during design, enabling improved model-driven development of Digital Twins, and, eventually, fostering verification~\&~validation of Digital Twins by delivering a model-based foundation for test case inference.

### [204] [A Scalable Benchmark for Repository-Oriented Long-Horizon Conversational Context Management](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06358)
*Yang Liu,Li Zhang,Fang Liu,Ping Lin,Xinyi Li*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: LoCoEval是首个针对仓库开发场景的长对话上下文管理基准，通过LLM驱动流程生成真实多样的仓库导向对话，评估现有方法表现并提出改进方案


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型在代码理解和生成方面进步显著，但在实际仓库开发中，过长的对话上下文可能导致关键信息丢失和性能下降。现有上下文管理方法主要针对通用对话，缺乏针对仓库开发场景的解决方案和可靠评估基准

Method: 提出LoCoEval基准，遵循三个关键原则，通过LLM驱动流程生成真实多样的仓库导向对话，捕捉迭代需求、噪声输入和回顾性提问等关键交互模式。评估了7个基线方法（包括4种代表性上下文管理方法），使用3种先进骨干LLM

Conclusion: LoCoEval填补了仓库开发场景中长对话上下文管理评估的空白，揭示了现有方法的局限性，提出的改进方法表现出色，为未来研究提供了可操作的见解

Abstract: In recent years, large language models (LLMs) have advanced rapidly, substantially enhancing their code understanding and generation capabilities and giving rise to powerful code assistants. However, in practical repository development, excessively long-horizon conversational context may overwhelm models, causing the loss of critical information and degraded performance, thereby limiting the utility of code assistants. Existing context management methods proposed to mitigate this context dilemma primarily target general-purpose conversations, while repository-oriented solutions remain largely unexplored, which is largely due to the lack of reliable evaluation benchmarks. To bridge this gap, we present LoCoEval, the first long-horizon conversational context management benchmark tailored to repository-oriented development scenarios. Adhering to three key principles, LoCoEval is constructed via an LLM-driven pipeline that generates realistic and diverse repository-oriented conversations, capturing key interaction patterns such as iterative requirements, noisy input, and retrospective questions. We evaluate 7 baselines, including 4 representative context management methods, using 3 advanced backbone LLMs on LoCoEval. The results reveal substantial challenges faced by standalone LLMs and existing approaches, especially memory systems, in repository-oriented conversational scenarios. To address these limitations, we further propose an improved method integrating conversational and repository information into a unified memory, which outperforms all baselines (*Oracle* excluded) and demonstrates robustness. Additionally, we investigated the impact of various factors on method performance, providing actionable insights for future research.

</details>


### [205] [A Reference Architecture of Reinforcement Learning Frameworks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06413)
*Xiaoran Liu,Istvan David*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出强化学习框架的参考架构，通过分析18个实践框架识别核心组件和关系，为框架比较、评估和集成提供共同基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前强化学习框架的架构模式在实现中不一致，缺乏统一的参考架构来支持框架的比较、评估和集成。

Method: 采用扎根理论方法分析18个先进的实践RL框架，识别重复出现的架构组件及其关系，并将其编码为参考架构。

Result: 提出了RL框架的参考架构，通过重构特征性RL模式进行验证，识别了架构趋势（如常用组件），并指出了改进RL框架的路径。

Conclusion: 提出的参考架构为RL框架提供了共同比较基础，有助于促进框架评估、集成和未来发展。

Abstract: The surge in reinforcement learning (RL) applications gave rise to diverse supporting technology, such as RL frameworks. However, the architectural patterns of these frameworks are inconsistent across implementations and there exists no reference architecture (RA) to form a common basis of comparison, evaluation, and integration. To address this gap, we propose an RA of RL frameworks. Through a grounded theory approach, we analyze 18 state-of-the-practice RL frameworks and, by that, we identify recurring architectural components and their relationships, and codify them in an RA. To demonstrate our RA, we reconstruct characteristic RL patterns. Finally, we identify architectural trends, e.g., commonly used components, and outline paths to improving RL frameworks.

</details>


### [206] [Understanding and Finding JIT Compiler Performance Bugs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06551)
*Zijian Yi,Cheng Ding,August Shi,Milos Gligoric*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 首个针对JIT编译器性能bug的系统研究，通过实证分析发现常见模式，并提出分层差分性能测试方法Jittery，成功检测出12个新bug。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JIT编译器是许多流行编程语言的关键组件，但现有研究主要关注功能bug检测，缺乏对性能bug的系统研究。性能bug会导致运行时显著性能下降，但由于JIT编译器的复杂性和动态性，检测这些bug具有挑战性。

Method: 1. 对Java和JavaScript的四个流行JIT编译器进行实证研究，手动分析191个bug报告，总结性能bug的常见触发因素、表现模式和根本原因；2. 基于这些洞察，提出分层差分性能测试方法，并实现工具Jittery；3. 在Jittery中集成测试优先级排序（减少92.40%测试时间）和自动过滤误报/重复项等优化。

Result: 1. 通过实证研究揭示了JIT性能bug的模式和原因；2. Jittery在Oracle HotSpot和Graal JIT编译器中发现了12个先前未知的性能bug，其中11个得到开发者确认，6个已被修复；3. 测试优先级排序使测试时间减少92.40%，同时保持bug检测能力。

Conclusion: 这是首个系统研究JIT编译器性能bug的工作，提出的分层差分性能测试方法Jittery能有效检测性能bug，实证结果证明了其有效性，为JIT编译器质量保障提供了新工具。

Abstract: Just-in-time (JIT) compilers are key components for many popular programming languages with managed runtimes (e.g., Java and JavaScript). JIT compilers perform optimizations and generate native code at runtime based on dynamic profiling data, to improve the execution performance of the running application. Like other software systems, JIT compilers might have software bugs, and prior work has developed a number of automated techniques for detecting functional bugs (i.e., generated native code does not semantically match that of the original code). However, no prior work has targeted JIT compiler performance bugs, which can cause significant performance degradation while an application is running. These performance bugs are challenging to detect due to the complexity and dynamic nature of JIT compilers. In this paper, we present the first work on demystifying JIT performance bugs. First, we perform an empirical study across four popular JIT compilers for Java and JavaScript. Our manual analysis of 191 bug reports uncovers common triggers of performance bugs, patterns in which these bugs manifest, and their root causes. Second, informed by these insights, we propose layered differential performance testing, a lightweight technique to automatically detect JIT compiler performance bugs, and implement it in a tool called Jittery. We incorporate practical optimizations into Jittery such as test prioritization, which reduces testing time by 92.40% without compromising bug-detection capability, and automatic filtering of false-positives and duplicates, which substantially reduces manual inspection effort. Using Jittery, we discovered 12 previously unknown performance bugs in the Oracle HotSpot and Graal JIT compilers, with 11 confirmed and 6 fixed by developers.

</details>
